# Beckhoff ELM3704-0001

ELM3704-0001 4Ch. Ana. Input +/-60V, +/-20mA, TC, RTD, Bridge Measuring (SG), IEPE, 24 bit, high precision, LEMO

Beckhoff Automation GmbH & Co. KG

http://www.beckhoff.com/ELM3704-0001
